Grand Prix Toronto Archetype Exemplars
======================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on May 4, 2015 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/hero/wizardslogo_thumb.jpg)
By Josh Bennett and Marc Calderaro











We all know you guys are hungering for more decklists. Being the benevolent people we are, here are lots of them.  Here are the top-finishing player in each given archetype from Day 2 of Grand Prix Toronto. Some of them might seem like splitting hairs, but we'd rather hedge on getting you more decklists than fewer. Enjoy.
